|Naming Nomenclature
All models follow the following naming method:
<family>_<I/O Standard>_<I/O>_<Features>

where,
<family> refers to: 
max7kb - MAX7000B device
max7kae - MAX7000AE device

<I/O Standard> refers to:
ttl25 - 2.5V LVTTL/LVCMOS
sstl33 - 3.3V SSTL 

<I/O> refers to:
io  - I/O
in  - input

<Features> refers to:
s   - Slow slew rate

Example: max7kb_ttl33_io_s refers to
Max7000B, 3.3V LVTTL/LVCMOS I/O model with Slow Slew Rate
